    <string name="saver_getting_results_explanation">"After you scan your store receipt, it typically takes 2–3 days for Savings Catcher to notify you with your results. During that time, Savings Catcher works with a third party to find and review nearby top retailers' weekly ads, both the print and online versions. Savings Catcher then looks for ads that match the eligible items on your receipt and compares these advertised prices against the prices you paid at Walmart. To be a match, the advertised items must be of identical size, quantity, brand, flavor, and color to your Walmart items, and the ads must be valid at the time you made your purchase. Gathering and reviewing this amount of data takes some time. We are working to speed up this process."</string>
